# 性能测试样例 — perf-mixed

约 400KB 混合内容：段落、代码块、5 个 Mermaid 图表。

```mermaid
flowchart TB
    subgraph 客户端
        A[用户] --> B[打开文档]
    end
    subgraph 处理
        B --> C[解析] --> D[HTML] --> E[首帧]
        C --> F[Mermaid 异步]
    end
```

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant U as 用户
    participant C as Controller
    U->>C: openFile
    alt OK
        C-->>U: 展示
    else ERR
        C-->>U: 错误
    end
```

```mermaid
classDiagram
    Animal <|-- Dog
    class Animal { +name }
    class Dog { +bark() }
```

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> 空闲
    state 加载 {
        [*] --> 解析 --> 布局
    }
    空闲 --> 加载 --> 完成
```

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    A --> B --> C
```
